{\footnotesize\ttfamily D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+A\+C\+F\+U\+ID (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x_8h_ab19414382287ff80930c48a196145214}{acf\+U\+ID}}}]{,  }\item[{A\+C\+F\+A\+T\+T\+R\+\_\+\+Param\+Definition\+\_\+\+Default\+Component\+Order}]{,  }\item[{0x27995d37}]{,  }\item[{0x50aa}]{,  }\item[{0x00b4}]{,  }\item[{0xb4}]{,  }\item[{0x58}]{,  }\item[{0x08}]{,  }\item[{0x96}]{,  }\item[{0x02}]{,  }\item[{0xdc}]{,  }\item[{0xb9}]{,  }\item[{0x6d}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Used to define the mapping of the structure members to the default layout order for built-\/in Point2D, Rect2D, Color\+H\+SV and Color\+R\+GB. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
To be compatible with the layouts for A\+VX 1.\+x parameters the values for the built-\/in types are
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Point2D\+: \{0, 1\},
\item Rect2D \+: \{1, 0, 3, 2\},
\item Color\+H\+SV \+: \{0, 1, 2\}, and
\item Color\+R\+GB \+: \{0, 1, 2\}. ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ type\+: }} Int32\+Array ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ method\+: }}I\+A\+V\+X\+Parameter\+Definition; ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ context\+: }} parameter definition ~\newline
~\newline
 {\bfseries{ A\+VX Namespace name\+: }} com.\+avid.\+fx.\+param.\+attr.\+defaultcomponentorder ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ U\+ID String\+: }} 27995d37-\/50aa-\/36ec-\/b458-\/089602dcb96d 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Used to define the step value of a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_u_i}{UI}} widget ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ type\+: }} as defined by A\+C\+F\+A\+T\+T\+R\+\_\+\+Param\+Definition\+\_\+\+Data\+Type\+ID ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ method\+: }}I\+A\+V\+X\+Parameter\+Definition; ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ context\+: }} parameter definition ~\newline
~\newline
 {\bfseries{ A\+C\+F\+Namespace name\+: }} com.\+avid.\+fx.\+param.\+attr.\+increment ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ U\+ID String\+: }} The default is 1.\+0. It is used to define the stepping value of a slider. You can use it to set the stepping value of a slider or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_u_i}{UI}} widget. For example a value of 0.\+1 on a slider with a range from 0-\/100 will Have slider drag the slider with values 20.\+1, 20.\+2 ... as opposed to a default of 1.\+0 where the values would go 20.\+0, 21.\+0, 22.\+0 .... A value of 2.\+0 would go 20, 22, 24 etc. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+A\+C\+F\+U\+ID (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x_8h_ab19414382287ff80930c48a196145214}{acf\+U\+ID}}}]{,  }\item[{A\+C\+F\+A\+T\+T\+R\+\_\+\+Param\+Definition\+\_\+\+Need\+Accumulation\+Buffer}]{,  }\item[{0xb5d3b187}]{,  }\item[{0x84a9}]{,  }\item[{0x46ec}]{,  }\item[{0xb5}]{,  }\item[{0xd3}]{,  }\item[{0xd7}]{,  }\item[{0x7c}]{,  }\item[{0xe2}]{,  }\item[{0x63}]{,  }\item[{0x28}]{,  }\item[{0x73}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
A hidden parameter that indicates whether or not an effect internally uses an accumulation buffer so that the results of one frame depend on the results of previous frames. A True value signifies that the effect must always be fully rendered in one atomic operation, while a False value (the default) means the effect is allowed to be partially rendered. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
FX should not create this parameter themselves, but only get access to it via a \char`\"{}find\char`\"{} or \char`\"{}get\char`\"{} mechanism instead. ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ type\+: }} Boolean ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ method\+: }}I\+A\+V\+X\+Parameter\+Definition; ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ context\+: }} parameter definition ~\newline
~\newline
 {\bfseries{ A\+VX Namespace name\+: }} ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ U\+ID String\+: }} B5\+D3\+B187-\/84\+A9-\/46\+E\+C-\/\+B5\+D3-\/\+D77\+C\+E2632873 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{acfuids_8h_a884e3691cb57c135f248353141a25066}\label{acfuids_8h_a884e3691cb57c135f248353141a25066}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+A\+C\+F\+U\+ID (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x_8h_ab19414382287ff80930c48a196145214}{acf\+U\+ID}}}]{,  }\item[{A\+C\+F\+A\+T\+T\+R\+\_\+\+Param\+Definition\+\_\+\+U\+I\+Precision}]{,  }\item[{0x83bcd82e}]{,  }\item[{0x133d}]{,  }\item[{0x0082}]{,  }\item[{0x82}]{,  }\item[{0xb6}]{,  }\item[{0xcd}]{,  }\item[{0x45}]{,  }\item[{0xca}]{,  }\item[{0x5f}]{,  }\item[{0x74}]{,  }\item[{0x24}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Used to define the precision to display the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_u_i}{UI}} value. This optional attribute Used to override the display precision for double parameters. This is valid to 0 to display double parameters as integers. A special value of -\/1 (the default) indicates that the host should use its standard precision for displaying doubles. ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ type\+: }} acf\+S\+Int32 ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ method\+: }}I\+A\+V\+X\+Parameter\+Definition; ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ context\+: }} parameter definition ~\newline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+A\+C\+F\+U\+ID (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x_8h_ab19414382287ff80930c48a196145214}{acf\+U\+ID}}}]{,  }\item[{A\+C\+F\+Comp\+I\+D\+\_\+\+Host\+Memory\+Allocator}]{,  }\item[{0xc97930cf}]{,  }\item[{0xfbb8}]{,  }\item[{0x4789}]{,  }\item[{0xaf}]{,  }\item[{0x19}]{,  }\item[{0x51}]{,  }\item[{0xd4}]{,  }\item[{0xc2}]{,  }\item[{0x25}]{,  }\item[{0x59}]{,  }\item[{0xc0}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
A\+V\+X\+Component\+I\+D\+\_\+\+Host\+Memeory\+Allocator This is the component id used for the host memory allocator. All memory allocated with this component will be from the host\textquotesingle{}s memory address space. Use this object to allocate dynamic buffers for plug-\/ins. The plug-\/in could also override the global C++ new function in the plug-\/in so that all C++ objects can use the same host memory allocator (this will require implementing the A\+C\+F\+Startup and A\+C\+F\+Shutdown callbacks).
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The host memory allocator is implemented by the host it is accessed through the I\+A\+C\+F\+Malloc interface with I\+ID equal to I\+I\+D\+\_\+\+I\+A\+C\+F\+Malloc (see acfmemory.\+h). ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ type\+: }} U\+I\+DS; ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ method\+: }}Create\+Component; ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ context\+: }} global ~\newline
~\newline
 {\bfseries{ A\+C\+F\+Namespace name\+: }} ~\newline
 {\bfseries{ U\+ID String\+: }} 
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
A component may encounter this data type on older hosts that did not have any support for persisting A\+C\+F\+Type\+I\+D\+\_\+\+U\+T\+F16\+String data. This type is reserved for host applications and should never be used in any definition by a plug-\/in. Newer plug-\/ins should be written to either fail gracefully or convert the returned U\+T\+F8 as necessary. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
